2014-01-24 18:48:11,331 [7872] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode
2014-01-24 18:48:16,150 [6576] DEBUG Sys - 
select 1
from sys_roleMenuMap A
left join sys_userRoleMap B on B.RoleCode = A.RoleCode
left join sys_menu C on C.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.UserCode = 'super'
and C.URL in ('/Sys/generator/Index','/Sys/generator')

2014-01-24 19:00:00,216 [6876] DEBUG Sys - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2014-01-24 19:27:06,146 [10380] DEBUG Sys - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('sys_log')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2014-01-24 19:40:46,696 [10396] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('sys_log')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色

	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2014-01-24 20:30:18,185 [3932] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2014-01-24 22:29:11,871 [9996] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2014-01-24 22:30:26,950 [9876] DEBUG Sys - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('sys_log')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid

						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns

--角色的菜单

from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色

	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)

SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2014-01-24 23:31:20,798 [14744] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

from sys_button A

where B.UserCode = 'super'
)
order by ButtonSeq

2014-01-24 23:43:44,786 [14636] DEBUG Sys - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('sys_user')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id
